<div id="review_548300380" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/548300380" />
    <a title="AJ" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3143126-aj"><img alt="AJ" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1406382884p2/3143126.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/548300380?book_show_action=true">Feb 27, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="AJ" class="user" itemprop="url" name="AJ" href="/user/show/3143126-aj">AJ</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=series">series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=drama">drama</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=steamy">steamy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=pb-i-own">pb-i-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=romantic">romantic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=sob-fest">sob-fest</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer548300380" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18268951260351489083">Ummmmm… WTF just happened? Honestly, that’s pretty much the only thought my brain can process right now. But *pulls up the big girl panties* more of that later… <br/><br/><b>First and foremost, this is the conclusion to Woods and Della’s story, and it is an emotional, angsty, romantic, and really freaking steamy ride.</b><br/><br/>I love Woods! He is deeply, madly, and completely in love with Della, and is still swoony as all hell. But I must say, he almost seems a bit obsessed with her, unable to function without her clo</span>
  <span id="freeText18268951260351489083" style="display:none">Ummmmm… WTF just happened? Honestly, that’s pretty much the only thought my brain can process right now. But *pulls up the big girl panties* more of that later… <br /><br /><b>First and foremost, this is the conclusion to Woods and Della’s story, and it is an emotional, angsty, romantic, and really freaking steamy ride.</b><br /><br />I love Woods! He is deeply, madly, and completely in love with Della, and is still swoony as all hell. But I must say, he almost seems a bit obsessed with her, unable to function without her close, and smothering her with his love and protectiveness. <br /><br /><i>“In all her twisted perfection she had made me fall helplessly in love with her. A life without her in it seemed pointless.” </i><br /><br />Della is accepting of Woods’ smothering, so in love with her man that she is happy to do whatever she can to help him, and I love that she takes the initiative to be there for him and try to prove that she is capable despite Woods treating her like she’s made of glass. She still worries about her future, and her concerns about not being worthy of Woods continues to plague her. And this brings us to her moment of epic stupid. Seriously, I rolled my eyes and was groaning my frustration as my pet peeves reared their heads again – stupid heroines jumping to conclusions and lack of communication. Ugh! But, I did like the way it was resolved. I like that it all got dealt with, I like that she was able to look back and realise what she had done was stupid, and I like that it led to some big changes for her. She needed to do it, I just wish she’d handled it a bit differently. And I have to say, I love the way that Woods dealt with it! Just more proof of his awesomeness!<br /><br />And it’s not just Della going through changes, Woods’ life has completely changed since the last book, and although it is unexpected, he is embracing his new role and responsibilities and claiming it as his own, and I loved that! He is all badass and ‘take charge’ with what he wants, and it was great watching him.<br /><br />There’s a lot of stuff going on personally for both Della and Woods, but the love between them is never in doubt, and I love their romance. They are from completely different worlds, but they have an incredible love story, and they are so intensely passionate about each other! The sex scenes in this book are scorching, and then Woods comes out with the dirty talk, and it’s just… Whoa!<br /><br />I love the ongoing involvement of the other characters in this series, and we get to see a lot of them in this one. Tripp, Jace, Bethy, Della’s awesome friend Braden, and of course, Rush, Blaire and Grant, and even Rush’s Dad, Dean, make appearances! I loved getting to see where everybody is at, and the scenes where they are all together are just gold.<br /><br />There are some big developments for the rest of the series - Grant is in a clusterfuck, with some seriously big stuff going on with him (enough with the Nan storyline! Seriously! Just, no!). And Tripp gets a fair bit of story time, which is great because I love him! There are some huge reveals for him, and I now assume he’ll be getting a book of his own, and all I can say is… DAMN!<br /><br />And then there’s that twist. OMG! Out of nowhere, my mind was blown and I can’t believe Abbi went there! I was in total and utter shock, and had tears streaming down my face. The emotion! OMG it was intense! <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ And I just have to say, I HATE that she wrote it, but I hate even more that she put it so late in the story! I was so gutted, and then so shocked by the next big reveal, that when Woods and Della got their HEA, I was still trapped in my emotion from a couple of chapters previously. Seriously. WTF was that? I’m sitting here writing this review, and all I can see in my head is that scene where the boys are all on the beach staring out over the water. I’m still depressed beyond belief. Just… WHYYYYYYYYYYYYYYYYYYYYYY??? *sob* <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />But despite the questionable ending, I really enjoyed this book. I thought it was really well written, and (love it or hate it) Abbi does a great job bringing the emotion, I was really feeling this one! In fact, I was feeling it so much that it took away some of the happiness from Woods and Della’s HEA, which was a bit disappointing. But I still loved their story. Yes, the characters did things that annoyed me at times, but it was important to their journey, and it all builds beautifully to a very satisfying HEA.<br /><br />4 stars. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="18268951260351489083" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer966477528923229214">3.5 Stars<br/><br/><a href='http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/image_zps8e426b59.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380412045i/810071._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo image_zps8e426b59.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Well, what can I say about "Simple Perfection"?<br/>I felt like we waited an eternity for its release date.<br/>I really loved "Twisted Perfection"!!<br/>Woods was so very alpha, beautiful & swoon worthy.<br/><br/>While reading this book, I kept asking myself "where did my Woods go?!!"<br/>He was extremely sappy at times.<br/>I loved how he was "all in" with Della but it was like he lost his manhood!!<br/>He won points with me for always putting Della first but he was a bit smothering.<br/>Even with him being on top of Della a</span>
  <span id="freeText966477528923229214" style="display:none">3.5 Stars<br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/image_zps8e426b59.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380412045i/810071._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo image_zps8e426b59.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Well, what can I say about "Simple Perfection"?<br>I felt like we waited an eternity for its release date.<br>I really loved "Twisted Perfection"!!<br>Woods was so very alpha, beautiful &amp; swoon worthy.<br><br>While reading this book, I kept asking myself "where did my Woods go?!!"<br>He was extremely sappy at times.<br>I loved how he was "all in" with Della but it was like he lost his manhood!!<br>He won points with me for always putting Della first but he was a bit smothering.<br>Even with him being on top of Della almost 24/7, stupid Angelina and his mother still get their claws in her.<br>I wanted to scream at Della to beat the ever loving crap out of Angelina!!!<br>Why did she have to be so weak?!!!!!<br><br>There are some big revelations for Della, which I thought were so "convenient" to the story and angst ensues that has Woods and Della separated for a bit.<br><br><i>
  <b>"When she left here she took my soul with her. I will always belong to her. I don't want her to ever think differently."</b>
</i> - Woods<br><br>Then BAM @ 84% into the story, we're hit with shit way out of left field!!!<br>I DID NOT SEE THAT COMING!!!<br>Holy shit I still feel so bad!!<br>God damn Abbi you could have went a different route with that story!!<br>Possible angst filled "love triangle" there. I know how people just love them some ❤️ triangles!! LOL<br><br>So Woods is so head over heels, lovesick puppy dog for Della and I was asking myself, so what's the big hold up with taking the next step????<br><br><i>
  <b>"You're my all-in, Della. I'll throw it all away for you. I just want you. I'm all in, baby. This life with you, I'm planning on us."</b>
</i> - Woods<br><br>I don't think this was as good as the first book and Woods lost some of his edge, but I still love him.<br>He sure had a dirty mouth in this one. So hot during the sex scenes, which I could have had some more of, by the way!!!<br>I'm hoping that we get at least another book to finish Della &amp; Woods' story.<br><br>I also am anxious to read Trip's story.<br>Gonna be very interesting, given what went down.<br><br>So I gave this one 3.5 stars because although I didn't love it, it had its moments and was an enjoyable read. ☺️</span>

<div id="review_709407963" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/709407963?book_show_action=true">Sep 01, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Len" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Len" href="/user/show/12260723-len">Len</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12260723-len?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12260723-len?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12260723-len?shelf=boss-in-love">boss-in-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12260723-len?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12260723-len?shelf=uber-controlling-hero">uber-controlling-hero</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer709407963" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1273683056250767517">This is me on released date and want to start reading it asap<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380433573ra/872587.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380435181ra/879162.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i>Simple Perfection</i> is a beautiful inspiring story. It's about being strong,loving unselfishly, forgiving,understanding,and acceptance. I like the plot of the story but somehow some of it didn't work for me. I'm not disappointed but it didn't amused me either. This was a sad,emotional read though you can't put it down. <br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380435181ra/879163.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i>What i like</i><br/>I like Della so much. I like how she overcome her past and bad memories. Indeed she was a very strong woman. </span>
  <span id="freeText1273683056250767517" style="display:none">This is me on released date and want to start reading it asap<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380433573ra/872587.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380435181ra/879162.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>Simple Perfection</i> is a beautiful inspiring story. It's about being strong,loving unselfishly, forgiving,understanding,and acceptance. I like the plot of the story but somehow some of it didn't work for me. I'm not disappointed but it didn't amused me either. This was a sad,emotional read though you can't put it down. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380435181ra/879163.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>What i like</i><br>I like Della so much. I like how she overcome her past and bad memories. Indeed she was a very strong woman. I like how understanding she was. She was determined to proved herself worthy of Woods. <br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <i>“With Woods arms wrapped around me and the beat of his heart pressed against my chest, I knew he would hold me steady. If I ever fell, I’d have him to catch me.”</i>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>Woods, I love him more in this book. I love how protective,patient,loving and possessive he was to Della. He was definitely hot alpha male. I love him more for what he did to Della when she went looking for herself. Oh and I love how sweet he is. For Woods alone i can give five stars for this book.<br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <i>"Hold her for me. Hold her tight. Don't let her be lonely. Don't let her hurt"<br><br>"I stayed away because I wanted you to come back to me. I wanted you to want me. To want us."<br><br>"In all her twisted perfection she had made me fall helplessly in love with her. A life without her in it seemed pointless."</i>
  </blockquote>
</b> <br>This was also intense,steamy hot read. Though the sex scene is not so much,which I'm glad but it will definitely leave you fanning yourself. This two is like a time bomb,when they have their together,they explode.they will make you throw your panty away.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380435181ra/879164.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380393662ra/757963.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>There were some unexpected scene <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Jace save Bethy that caused his life <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> that really broke my heart. The author did well in that part. That twist I didn't see coming.<br><i>What didn't work for me</i><br>I understand this is Woods and Della story,but why there are some side stories came out. I'm interested in their stories, but they should have their own.Just saying. I want to know too what happened to crazy mother and selfish spoiled bitch Angelina. I felt their happy ending lack of something. Just saying again.</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer548174033" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9482273310168412870">It was great to be back in Rosemary Beach with Woods, Rush, Jace, and the rest of the gang! It’s official, Woods is definitely my favorite. He may have grown up as a rich and spoiled trust fund brat, but he seems to be the only one of his friends with an actual job. After his father’s unexpected death, Woods has taken over the Kerrington Club. <br/><br/>At 25, he is carrying on his grandfather’s legacy. He’s firing the current board of directors and surrounding himself with people that he trusts. This doe</span>
  <span id="freeText9482273310168412870" style="display:none">It was great to be back in Rosemary Beach with Woods, Rush, Jace, and the rest of the gang! It’s official, Woods is definitely my favorite. He may have grown up as a rich and spoiled trust fund brat, but he seems to be the only one of his friends with an actual job. After his father’s unexpected death, Woods has taken over the Kerrington Club. <br /><br />At 25, he is carrying on his grandfather’s legacy. He’s firing the current board of directors and surrounding himself with people that he trusts. This does not include his crazy mother (who does not approve of Della) or his crazy ex-fiance (who is trying to scare Della off so she can have Woods back).<br /><br />In typical Abbi Glines-style, there is lots of drama and lots of miscommunication. Woods is still his overprotective caveman self, but I loved him. He is so enamored with Della. <br /><blockquote>
  <i>“She was my go-all-in,” I said as I stared down at the smashed-up bar stool.<br /><br />“Your what?” Jace asked.<br /><br />“Della was my go-all-in. She was my winning hand. You can’t play when you go all in and lose. I’m out.”<br /><br />“No, you’re not. This hand ain’t over yet,” Rush said.</i>
</blockquote><br />Della is still in need of someone to shake some sense into her, but she does finally come around during the latter part of the book. She and Woods get their happily ever after and it’s very sweet. I loved the ending.</span>
  <a data-text-id="9482273310168412870" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_596932487" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/596932487" />
    <a title="Mary" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10394863-mary"><img alt="Mary" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1373463422p2/10394863.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/596932487?book_show_action=true">Apr 22, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mary" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mary" href="/user/show/10394863-mary">Mary</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer596932487" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7974905921119531392"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"You're my all-in, Della. I'll throw it all away for you. I just want you. I'm all in, baby.</i>
  </b>
  <br/>
  <br/>
</blockquote>***3.5 stars*** <br/><br/>I think I'm really developing a love-hate relationship with Abbi Glines' sequels. <b>Twisted Perfection</b> is my most favorite work of hers and Woods and Della are my favorite couple. I really thought that she stepped up her game with their story, especially dealing with Della's complicated and sensitive back story. Needless to say, I've been looking forward to getting the cont</span>
  <span id="freeText7974905921119531392" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"You're my all-in, Della. I'll throw it all away for you. I just want you. I'm all in, baby.</i>
  </b>
  <br />
  <br />
</blockquote>***3.5 stars*** <br /><br />I think I'm really developing a love-hate relationship with Abbi Glines' sequels. <b>Twisted Perfection</b> is my most favorite work of hers and Woods and Della are my favorite couple. I really thought that she stepped up her game with their story, especially dealing with Della's complicated and sensitive back story. Needless to say, I've been looking forward to getting the continuation to their story and it just saddens me a bit that instead of getting better, this story was kind of a letdown. And believe me, it actually hurts me to give a low rating to this one because it feels like I'm betraying Woods. (LOL)<br /><br />The story started out very weak and very irritating with the typical <i>"I'm-not-worthy-of-him-so-I'll-just-leave"</i> drama. It did pick up somewhere in the middle and I found myself really engaged in Della's thoughts and feelings as well as Woods' pain. I really understood the intention of the author to come up with a moving and inspirational story, especially concerning Della's condition, but I think it fell short on the actual delivery because the dialogues felt a bit robotic and unfeeling to me and the way the story progressed just didn't have much room for substance and depth. Another thing I felt a bit wary about the story was the huge twist towards the end that came out of nowhere. All it felt like was that she's building it up again for another spin-off with <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Bethy and Tripp... who would've guessed, right? <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> and the already established spin-off with Grant, Nan, and Harlow's story. <br /><br />I'll tell you this, though... Woods is as swoon-worthy as ever and I offer the three stars to him and .5 for Della finally coming to her senses. The thing with Abbi Glines book is that it just has this certain addicting factor that even if I feel the same way book after book, I still keep coming back for more. There were some moments that made me emotional and all fluttery on the inside and I wished there were more of those feeling moments between Della and Woods, instead of having WTF moments and side stories that veer away from the actual plot. Nevertheless, I still loved reading more about my favorite Abbi Glines couple and I'm not really sure if this is the last because even though it ended on a HEA, there's still room for <i>more</i>. I'm not saying it needs a third book but I'm almost sure that even though it wouldn't amount to anything that epic, I'd still read it anyway. Such is my love-hate relationship with Abbi Glines' sequels :)</span>
  <a data-text-id="7974905921119531392" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText15043162162082275347" style="display:none">I cannot believe this!!! I LOVED this installment of Woods and Della's story but damn if I wasn't pissed at 85%! Woods is a possessive alpha male to the max, but at the beginning his possessive more sounded like obsessive. His constant "I can't breathe without her" was a little much, but definitely showed how much he cared for her. Woods parents and their way of handling their son annoyed me. The rich and privileged only caring how others perceived them is such a waste of a human - I hate that he grew up like that, but glad he found real love and was able to show her his love. <br />Della had a lot of demons to work through but was able to overcome them herself so she could be the woman she thought Woods needed. <br />Ready for Tripp's book!!!!             Shelves:

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2191018056" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17084217052955350962">I have to say that I enjoyed the other book more <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2188955671?book_show_action=false&from_review_page=1' rel='nofollow noopener'>Twisted Perfection</a> but it was still pretty enjoyable. Unfortunately I had some issues with it. In my previous review I said that I like Della as a character, but now not so much. There is a difference between a character who has suffered through lot of messed up stuffed and a weak character. In the other book she was shown as strong, but with bad past and lots of stuff to work through. Here she was just weak. But I liked that around the end of the</span>
  <span id="freeText17084217052955350962" style="display:none">I have to say that I enjoyed the other book more <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2188955671?book_show_action=false&amp;from_review_page=1" rel="nofollow noopener">Twisted Perfection</a> but it was still pretty enjoyable. Unfortunately I had some issues with it. In my previous review I said that I like Della as a character, but now not so much. There is a difference between a character who has suffered through lot of messed up stuffed and a weak character. In the other book she was shown as strong, but with bad past and lots of stuff to work through. Here she was just weak. But I liked that around the end of the book she got a bit more confident.<br />Also Woods wasn't what he used to be. He used to be a cool, strong and fun character. Here he was needy and really overprotective. Don't even get me started on how he didn't let her out of the house, because he wanted her safe.<br />At some I actually liked that she ran away. Though I didn't like the reason for it. I sometimes think that every time, when an author is struggling with the plot, she writes some kind of misunderstanding. <br />A thing that also annoyed he was that they seemed to try to solve everything with sex. Evert time they had a problem, they were like lets just have sex. Why should we try to communicate<br />Another thing was Jase's dead. That was totally unnecessary. </span>

<div id="review_1739924882" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1739924882" />
    <a title="Elle&#39;s Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/44344367-elle-s-book-blog"><img alt="Elle&#39;s Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1601066023p2/44344367.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1739924882?book_show_action=true">Aug 26, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Elle&#39;s Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Elle&#39;s Book Blog" href="/user/show/44344367-elle-s-book-blog">Elle&#39;s Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44344367-elle-s-book-blog?shelf=romance">romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1739924882" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4527083557999637700"><b> Genre: </b> New Adult Romance<br/><b> Series: </b> The Rosemary Beach series (read Twisted Perfection prior to this one)<br/><br/><b> :: 4.5 Pretty Little Stars :: </b><br/><br/>Simple Perfection is another winner in Abbi Glines bestselling Rosemary Beach series. This one is also the conclusion to Della and Wood's story, so make sure you read Twisted Perfection first. Overall, I really enjoyed this book and it was great to see the how Della and Wood's relationship progressed after some startling discoveries. What I also like about these</span>
  <span id="freeText4527083557999637700" style="display:none"><b> Genre: </b> New Adult Romance<br /><b> Series: </b> The Rosemary Beach series (read Twisted Perfection prior to this one)<br /><br /><b> :: 4.5 Pretty Little Stars :: </b><br /><br />Simple Perfection is another winner in Abbi Glines bestselling Rosemary Beach series. This one is also the conclusion to Della and Wood's story, so make sure you read Twisted Perfection first. Overall, I really enjoyed this book and it was great to see the how Della and Wood's relationship progressed after some startling discoveries. What I also like about these two books in the series is that they deal with some heavy subjects; mainly mental health issues. It's nice to see that characters CAN have flaws and they are not all perfect. <br /><br />Readers who haven't read these books should be warned that this one in particular DOES contain a major plot twist. I ended up crying and wondering WHY Abbi would do this to us readers! Gosh, that was emotional. If your curious to se what I am talking about you'll have to read it! :p<br /><br />Anyway, this is a great book and even BETTER for those who read the entire series in order. While Twisted Perfection and Simple Perfection can standalone, it is recommended to read them in order because the characters from the other books (previous and future) are incorporated in them. So read the series if you haven't! I highly recommend them! :-)</span>
  <a data-text-id="4527083557999637700" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('5+inZMwPBGPZpoLP1+9PquKmbfeP6rv8UfmS9iK8AOjNJvVRX1/1qDvt39Luk5PrxcS9MhD+sgElh50RauORZw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('nXBT0R6h9dd/JWmHHv4L9lV8xVuAWUZZimadVbcIfaS3vgHkjfEEHJ1uNJongte3ch4Vnh9NT6T+GJKy/1fsKw==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer11860545960584130646">Abbi Glines is a #1 New York Times, USA Today, and Wall Street Journal bestselling author of the Rosemary Beach, Sea Breeze, Vincent Boys, Field Party and Existence series. She never cooks unless baking during the Christmas holiday counts. She believes in ghosts and has a habit of asking people if their house is haunted before she goes in it. She drinks afternoon tea because she wants to be Britis</span>
  <span id="freeText11860545960584130646" style="display:none">Abbi Glines is a #1 New York Times, USA Today, and Wall Street Journal bestselling author of the Rosemary Beach, Sea Breeze, Vincent Boys, Field Party and Existence series. She never cooks unless baking during the Christmas holiday counts. She believes in ghosts and has a habit of asking people if their house is haunted before she goes in it. She drinks afternoon tea because she wants to be British but alas she was born in Alabama. When asked how many books she has written she has to stop and count on her fingers. When she’s not locked away writing, she is reading, shopping (major shoe and purse addiction), sneaking off to the movies alone, and listening to the drama in her teenagers lives while making mental notes on the good stuff to use later. Don’t judge.<br /><br />You can connect with Abbi online in several different ways. She uses social media to procrastinate.<br /></span>
